[7915]
[7916]
- [[code/modules/docs|docs]] - The `docs` module serves as a centralized, code-free repository for project documentation and reference materials. It organizes knowledge into four sub-modules: `contracts` for CLI tool specifications and shared graph schemas, `guides` for comprehensive developer and user documentation across core subsystems, `plans` for archived development roadmaps and design specifications, and `spikes` for cross-language technical research. As a documentation-only collection, it provides architectural references, workflow guides, and historical design records without containing executable code or indexed API symbols.
- [[code/modules/scripts|scripts]] - The `scripts` module contains shell utilities for project automation, primarily featuring `verify.sh` for running verification checks. It does not expose any indexed API symbols or child components.
